focus_tree = {
	id = russia2_soviet_focus
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 300 y = 2000 }

	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 1000
			OR = {
				tag = SOV
				tag = SOJ
			}
		}
	}

	#The Second Five Year Plan
	focus = {
		id = SOV_start_five_year_plan
		x = 13
		y = 1
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_soviet_construction
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 8
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_full_control_of_state = ROOT.capital
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		completion_reward = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SOV_start_five_year_plan
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 2
				category = industry
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unhappy_peasants1
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_start_five_year_plans_tt2
			}
		}
	}

	#The Motherland
	focus = {
		id = SOV_the_motherland
		x = 13
		y = 2
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_start_five_year_plan }
		icon = GFX_The_motherland
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_idea = SOV_Russian_sphere_investments
			}
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
		completion_reward = {
			add_stability = 0.1
		}
	}

	#Begin the Infrastructure Project
	focus = {
		id = SOV_begin_infrastructure_project
		x = 3
		y = 2
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_start_five_year_plan }
		icon = GFX_focus_Railway
		cost = 8
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 7
		}
		available = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_war = yes }
				219 = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
			}
		}
		available_if_capitulated = yes
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_begin_infrastructure_project_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				219 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					build_railway = {
						level = 1
						build_only_on_allied = yes
						controller_priority = {
						  base = 1
						}
						fallback = yes
						start_state  = 219
						target_state = 242
					}
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_Infrastructure_problem
				add_idea = SOV_infrastructure_problem2
			}
		}
	}

			add_ideas = SOV_Home_of_perpetual_liberty
			create_faction = russian_sphere
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_create_russian_sphere_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_europe
							has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_asia
							has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_caucasus
						}
					}
					SOV = {
						# add_to_faction = PREV (not required)
						puppet = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = SOV_Unstable_government
						}
						remove_ideas = SOV_Unstable_government
					}
					add_ideas = SOV_Guided_by_russia
				}

				every_country = { #Making a second every_country to avoid confusing the PREV tag
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_europe
							has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_asia
							has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_caucasus
						}
					}
					SOV = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = PREV
							autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = newsrussia2.70 days = 1
				}
				country_event = {
					id = russia2_russia.264 days = 105
				}
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_the_track_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.430 days = 5 }
				set_variable = { SOV.sov_track_array_count = 0 }

				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = SOV.sov_track_array_count
							value = 10
							compare = less_than
						}
					}

					random_scope_in_array = {
						array = global.countries
						limit = {
							exists = yes
							any_state = {
								OR = {
									is_owned_by = THIS
									is_controlled_by = THIS
								}
								is_capital = yes
							}
							NOT = {
								tag = SOV
								has_civil_war = yes
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
								has_capitulated = yes
								has_war_with = SOV
								is_subject_of = SOV
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}

						add_to_array = { global.sov_track_available_states = THIS.capital }

						add_to_variable = { SOV.sov_track_array_count = 1 }
					}
				}

				random_scope_in_array = {
					array = global.sov_track_available_states
					limit = {}

					THIS = {
						set_state_flag = sov_stalin_hidding_state
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			has_government = democratic

				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_DEMOCRATIC_PREEMPTIVE_COUP_RUSSIA }
		completion_reward = {
			set_temp_variable = { communist_popularity_democratic = party_popularity@communism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { communist_popularity_democratic = -0.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { fascist_popularity_democratic = party_popularity@fascism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { fascist_popularity_democratic = -0.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { democratic_support_gain = 0 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { democratic_support_gain = party_popularity@communism }
			add_to_temp_variable = { democratic_support_gain = party_popularity@fascism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { democratic_support_gain = 0.25 }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = communist_popularity_democratic
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = fascist_popularity_democratic
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = democratic_support_gain
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Ban_extreme_political_elements_idea
		}
	}

				random_scope_in_array = {
					array = ROOT.owned_states
					limit = {

							is_in_array = { SOV.sov_democratic_investments_random_states = PREV }
						}
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 3
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}

					SOV = {
						add_to_array = { sov_democratic_investments_random_states = PREV }
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { loop_count = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	#The Destiny of Our Monarchy
	focus = {
		id = SOV_destiny_monarchy
		x = 50
		y = 22
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_restoration_tsar }
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_reintegrate_lost_state }
		icon = GFX_goal_tfv_strengthen_commonwealth_ties
		cost = 8
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 7
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = neutrality
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_NEUTRALITY_TSAR_RUSSIA FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER }
		completion_reward = {
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.509 days = 50 }
			}
			set_country_flag = sov_anna_anderston_can_return
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.212 days = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_destiny_monarchy_tt

			# 1 = opposed ; 2 = neutral ; 3 = support

			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 1 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 2 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 3 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 4 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 5 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 6 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 7 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 8 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 9 }
			add_to_array = { monarchy_houses_russia = 10 }

			set_variable = { houses_russia_half_index = 0 }
			for_each_loop = {
			    array = monarchy_houses_russia

			    add_to_variable = { houses_russia_half_index = 1 }
			}
			divide_variable = {
			    var = houses_russia_half_index
			    value = 2
			}

			set_variable = { house_russia_opposed = 0 }
			set_variable = { house_russia_neutral = 0 }
			set_variable = { house_russia_support = 0 }
			# set_variable = { debug_house_count = 0 }
			for_each_loop = {
			    array = monarchy_houses_russia
			    value = current
			    index = i

				set_temp_variable = { current_value = current }
				set_temp_variable = { current_index = i }
				set_variable = { house_russia^var:current_value = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
						    var = current_index
						    value = houses_russia_half_index
						    compare = less_than
						}
					}
					randomize_variable = {
						var = house_russia^var:current_value
						distribution = uniform
						min = 1
						max = 2
					}
				}
				else = {
					randomize_variable = {
						var = house_russia^var:current_value
						distribution = uniform
						min = 2
						max = 3
					}
				}
				round_variable = house_russia^var:current_value
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = house_russia^var:current_value
							value = 1
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current_value = 30 }
					add_to_variable = {
						var = house_russia_opposed
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = house_russia^var:current_value
							value = 2
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current_value = 20 }
					add_to_variable = {
						var = house_russia_neutral
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = house_russia^var:current_value
							value = 3
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current_value = 10 }
					add_to_variable = {
						var = house_russia_support
						value = 1
					}
				}
			    # add_to_variable = { debug_house_count = house_russia^var:current_value }
			}
		}
	}

	#The Anarchist Election
	focus = {
		id = SOV_anarchist_election
		x = 112
		y = 14
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_end_property_exploitataion_privilege focus = SOV_favor_common_ownership focus = SOV_abolish_wage_slavery }
		icon = GFX_focus_SOV_anarchist_election
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 7
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = anarchy
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANARCHY_PROCLAMATION_COMMUNE_RUSSIA }
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_anarchist_election_decision_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_justification_wargoal_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				create_ships_variant_for_anarchist_election = yes
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = anarchist_election_modifiers }
				set_variable_anarchist_election_to_0 = yes
				set_temp_variable = { current_party = 0 }
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = current_party
							value = sov_anarchist_election_parties^num
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { random_party_support = 0 }
					randomize_temp_variable = {
						var = random_party_support
						min = 0
						max = 100
						distribution = uniform
					}
					set_variable = { sov_anarchist_election_parties^var:current_party = random_party_support }
					add_to_temp_variable = { current_party = 1 }
				}
				find_highest_in_array = {
					array = sov_anarchist_election_parties
					index = sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party_temp
				}
				set_variable = { sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party = sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party_temp }
				set_variable_for_winning_anarchist_party_election = yes
			}
		}
	}

			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_ideas = SOV_Centralization_free_territories
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Spread Anarchism Beyond our Neighbors
	focus = {
		id = SOV_spread_anarchism_beyond_our_neighbors
		x = 125
		y = 15
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_centralization_free_territory }
		icon = GFX_Embrace_total_anarchy
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 7
		}
		available = {
			always = no
			is_subject = no
			has_government = anarchy
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANARCHY_TOTAL_ANARCHY_RUSSIA }
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = will_receive_wargoal_agains_minor_neighbor_nation
			custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_justification_wargoal_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								NOT = {
									is_in_faction_with = SOV
									TAG = SOV
									is_major = yes
									is_subject = yes
								}
								any_country = {
									is_neighbor_of = PREV
									is_in_faction_with = SOV
								}
							}
							AND = {
								is_neighbor_of = ROOT
								NOT = {
									is_in_faction_with = ROOT
									TAG = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						create_wargoal = {
							type = puppet_wargoal_focus
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Rebirth
	focus = {
		id = SOV_rebirth
		x = 118
		y = 20
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_spread_revolution_everywhere focus = SOV_spread_anarchism_beyond_our_neighbors }
		icon = GFX_goal_unknown_golden
		cost = 6
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		available = {
			always = no
			is_subject = no
			has_government = anarchy
			is_major = yes
			has_global_flag = sov_national_obligations_allowed
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_GOLDEN_FOCUS FOCUS_FILTER_ANARCHY_PROCLAMATION_COMMUNE_RUSSIA FOCUS_FILTER_ANARCHY_TOTAL_ANARCHY_RUSSIA }
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_rebirth_tt
			add_to_array = { sov_national_obligations_unlocked_indexes = 13 }
			set_variable = { sov_national_obligations_selected_index = 13 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = sov_unlocked_national_obligations
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = sov_unlocked_national_obligations
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = sov_open_national_obligations
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = sov_open_national_obligations
			}
		}
	}
}
